# Comments for Question 1, LLM=Grok 2 12-12

== Grader: Claude 3.7 Sonnet ==
  * grade_story_102.txt (grade=5.2)
    The mercenary's spinelessness is established but his character arc from cowardice to courage feels rushed and predictable. His motivation to "hush a prophecy" lacks specificity and emotional weight. The character's internal transformation happens too easily without meaningful struggle, making his development feel unearned. There's potential in the concept of a fallen hero seeking redemption, but the execution lacks psychological depth and nuance.

  * grade_story_0.txt (grade=5.2)
    Eliot's sheepish nature and analytical creativity are mentioned but not deeply explored. His motivation to charm the monster is clear, but his emotional journey lacks nuance. The character remains somewhat flat, with traits told rather than shown through meaningful actions or internal conflict. His relationship with the monster develops too easily, without sufficient tension or character growth.

  * grade_story_1.txt (grade=4.2)
    The character's phobias are mentioned but never specified, creating a vague rather than vivid portrayal. Alex's motivation "to dance on the edge of madness" feels disconnected from his actions of unraveling knots. The stunt double profession is merely stated without influencing the character's decisions or abilities. There's no meaningful character arc beyond a generic "conquering fears" resolution that feels unearned.

  * grade_story_103.txt (grade=4.2)
    The knight's "grudgingly sweet" nature is mentioned but never demonstrated through action or dialogue. His motivation to "hush the final cry of regret" lacks specificity and emotional depth. The character remains a vague archetype rather than a fully realized individual with clear internal conflicts. His reactions to the brass knocker and pattern are described but fail to reveal meaningful aspects of his personality.

  * grade_story_104.txt (grade=6.2)
    The steward's stoic nature and motivation to expose truth are established, but his character lacks depth and specificity. His dedication to "uncovering cracks in the façade" is stated rather than demonstrated through meaningful actions or internal conflict. The character remains somewhat abstract, with limited personal details or distinctive voice that would make him memorable.

  * grade_story_100.txt (grade=6.2)

Her reactions to discoveries remain somewhat generic, missing opportunities for genuine character revelation through specific emotional responses.
